We finished the quarter with another record number of users reaching 570 million MAUs globally, reflecting 10% growth year-over-year. At the same time, we generated Q1 revenue of $855 million up 16% year-over-year due to the strong performance we are driving for advertisers across the full funnel. This is an indication that our efforts to build a more engaging and actionable product for our users and a more performant product for our advertisers are working. As we've made our platform more actionable and generated growing numbers of clicks and conversions, we've become a vital partner for advertisers across a range of categories seeking to reach our high intent users and drive sales. Revenue from Rest of World was $45 million, growing 49% on a reported basis or 59% on a constant currency basis.
